       'taskquery' => 'SELECT CONCAT( \'lawyersys/officalletter-edit?id=\', jomiz_jsys_lawyersys_officalletter.id ) AS task_link, jomiz_jsys_lawyersys_officalletter.recipient AS task_title, \'اضافة مرفق\' AS action_title, jomiz_jsys_lawyersys_officalletter.letter_date AS created_on, \'danger\' AS action_color from jomiz_jsys_lawyersys_officalletter LEFT OUTER JOIN jomiz_jsys_heap_attachments ON ( jomiz_jsys_lawyersys_officalletter.id = jomiz_jsys_heap_attachments.object_id AND jomiz_jsys_heap_attachments.object_type = \'officalletter\') GROUP by jomiz_jsys_lawyersys_officalletter.id HAVING count(jomiz_jsys_heap_attachments.id) = 0',

       'taskquery' => 'SELECT \'lawyersys/leavesapprovals\' AS task_link, jomiz_users.display_name AS task_title, \'مغادرة/إجازة\' AS action_title, jomiz_jsys_lawyersys_leaves_trs.start_date AS created_on, \'warning\' AS action_color FROM `jomiz_jsys_lawyersys_leaves_trs` INNER JOIN `jomiz_jsys_lawyersys_leave_types` on (`jomiz_jsys_lawyersys_leave_types`.id = `jomiz_jsys_lawyersys_leaves_trs`.`leave_type_id`) INNER JOIN jomiz_users on (jomiz_users.ID = `jomiz_jsys_lawyersys_leaves_trs`.`user_id`) WHERE `jomiz_jsys_lawyersys_leaves_trs`.taken > 0 AND `jomiz_jsys_lawyersys_leaves_trs`.`status` = 2 ORDER BY `start_date` ASC',
    ),
    1 => 
    (object) array(
       'permalink' => 'task-officalletter',
       'title' => 'Offical Letters',
       'template' => 'page-widget-task-officalletter.php',
       'istask' => true,
       'taskquery' => 'SELECT CONCAT( \'lawyersys/officalletter-edit?id=\', jomiz_jsys_lawyersys_officalletter.id ) AS task_link, jomiz_jsys_lawyersys_officalletter.recipient AS task_title, \'اضافة مرفق\' AS action_title, jomiz_jsys_lawyersys_officalletter.letter_date AS created_on, \'danger\' AS action_color from jomiz_jsys_lawyersys_officalletter LEFT OUTER JOIN jomiz_jsys_heap_attachments ON ( jomiz_jsys_lawyersys_officalletter.id = jomiz_jsys_heap_attachments.object_id AND jomiz_jsys_heap_attachments.object_type = \'officalletter\') GROUP by jomiz_jsys_lawyersys_officalletter.id HAVING count(jomiz_jsys_heap_attachments.id) = 0',
    ),
    2 => 
    (object) array(
       'permalink' => 'task-caseswithinweek',

       'taskquery' => 'SELECT \'lawyersys/leavesapprovals\' AS task_link, jomiz_users.display_name AS task_title, \'مغادرة/إجازة\' AS action_title, jomiz_jsys_lawyersys_leaves_trs.start_date AS created_on, \'warning\' AS action_color FROM `jomiz_jsys_lawyersys_leaves_trs` INNER JOIN `jomiz_jsys_lawyersys_leave_types` on (`jomiz_jsys_lawyersys_leave_types`.id = `jomiz_jsys_lawyersys_leaves_trs`.`leave_type_id`) INNER JOIN jomiz_users on (jomiz_users.ID = `jomiz_jsys_lawyersys_leaves_trs`.`user_id`) WHERE `jomiz_jsys_lawyersys_leaves_trs`.taken > 0 AND `jomiz_jsys_lawyersys_leaves_trs`.`status` = 2 ORDER BY `start_date` ASC',
    ),
    1 => 
    (object) array(
       'permalink' => 'task-officalletter',
       'title' => 'Offical Letters',
       'template' => 'page-widget-task-officalletter.php',
       'istask' => true,
       'taskquery' => 'SELECT CONCAT( \'lawyersys/officalletter-edit?id=\', jomiz_jsys_lawyersys_officalletter.id ) AS task_link, jomiz_jsys_lawyersys_officalletter.recipient AS task_title, \'اضافة مرفق\' AS action_title, jomiz_jsys_lawyersys_officalletter.letter_date AS created_on, \'danger\' AS action_color from jomiz_jsys_lawyersys_officalletter LEFT OUTER JOIN jomiz_jsys_heap_attachments ON ( jomiz_jsys_lawyersys_officalletter.id = jomiz_jsys_heap_attachments.object_id AND jomiz_jsys_heap_attachments.object_type = \'officalletter\') GROUP by jomiz_jsys_lawyersys_officalletter.id HAVING count(jomiz_jsys_heap_attachments.id) = 0',
    ),
    2 => 
    (object) array(
       'permalink' => 'task-caseswithinweek',

       'taskquery' => 'SELECT \'lawyersys/leavesapprovals\' AS task_link, jomiz_users.display_name AS task_title, \'مغادرة/إجازة\' AS action_title, jomiz_jsys_lawyersys_leaves_trs.start_date AS created_on, \'warning\' AS action_color FROM `jomiz_jsys_lawyersys_leaves_trs` INNER JOIN `jomiz_jsys_lawyersys_leave_types` on (`jomiz_jsys_lawyersys_leave_types`.id = `jomiz_jsys_lawyersys_leaves_trs`.`leave_type_id`) INNER JOIN jomiz_users on (jomiz_users.ID = `jomiz_jsys_lawyersys_leaves_trs`.`user_id`) WHERE `jomiz_jsys_lawyersys_leaves_trs`.taken > 0 AND `jomiz_jsys_lawyersys_leaves_trs`.`status` = 2 ORDER BY `start_date` ASC',
    ),
    1 => 
    (object) array(
       'permalink' => 'task-officalletter',
       'title' => 'Offical Letters',
       'template' => 'page-widget-task-officalletter.php',
       'istask' => true,
       'taskquery' => 'SELECT CONCAT( \'lawyersys/officalletter-edit?id=\', jomiz_jsys_lawyersys_officalletter.id ) AS task_link, jomiz_jsys_lawyersys_officalletter.recipient AS task_title, \'اضافة مرفق\' AS action_title, jomiz_jsys_lawyersys_officalletter.letter_date AS created_on, \'danger\' AS action_color from jomiz_jsys_lawyersys_officalletter LEFT OUTER JOIN jomiz_jsys_heap_attachments ON ( jomiz_jsys_lawyersys_officalletter.id = jomiz_jsys_heap_attachments.object_id AND jomiz_jsys_heap_attachments.object_type = \'officalletter\') GROUP by jomiz_jsys_lawyersys_officalletter.id HAVING count(jomiz_jsys_heap_attachments.id) = 0',
    ),
    2 => 
    (object) array(
       'permalink' => 'task-caseswithinweek',

       'taskquery' => 'SELECT \'lawyersys/leavesapprovals\' AS task_link, jomiz_users.display_name AS task_title, \'مغادرة/إجازة\' AS action_title, jomiz_jsys_lawyersys_leaves_trs.start_date AS created_on, \'warning\' AS action_color FROM `jomiz_jsys_lawyersys_leaves_trs` INNER JOIN `jomiz_jsys_lawyersys_leave_types` on (`jomiz_jsys_lawyersys_leave_types`.id = `jomiz_jsys_lawyersys_leaves_trs`.`leave_type_id`) INNER JOIN jomiz_users on (jomiz_users.ID = `jomiz_jsys_lawyersys_leaves_trs`.`user_id`) WHERE `jomiz_jsys_lawyersys_leaves_trs`.taken > 0 AND `jomiz_jsys_lawyersys_leaves_trs`.`status` = 2 ORDER BY `start_date` ASC',
    ),
    1 => 
    (object) array(
       'permalink' => 'task-officalletter',
       'title' => 'Offical Letters',
       'template' => 'page-widget-task-officalletter.php',
       'istask' => true,
       'taskquery' => 'SELECT CONCAT( \'lawyersys/officalletter-edit?id=\', jomiz_jsys_lawyersys_officalletter.id ) AS task_link, jomiz_jsys_lawyersys_officalletter.recipient AS task_title, \'اضافة مرفق\' AS action_title, jomiz_jsys_lawyersys_officalletter.letter_date AS created_on, \'danger\' AS action_color from jomiz_jsys_lawyersys_officalletter LEFT OUTER JOIN jomiz_jsys_heap_attachments ON ( jomiz_jsys_lawyersys_officalletter.id = jomiz_jsys_heap_attachments.object_id AND jomiz_jsys_heap_attachments.object_type = \'officalletter\') GROUP by jomiz_jsys_lawyersys_officalletter.id HAVING count(jomiz_jsys_heap_attachments.id) = 0',
    ),
    2 => 
    (object) array(
       'permalink' => 'task-caseswithinweek',

       'taskquery' => 'SELECT \'lawyersys/leavesapprovals\' AS task_link, jomiz_users.display_name AS task_title, \'مغادرة/إجازة\' AS action_title, jomiz_jsys_lawyersys_leaves_trs.start_date AS created_on, \'warning\' AS action_color FROM `jomiz_jsys_lawyersys_leaves_trs` INNER JOIN `jomiz_jsys_lawyersys_leave_types` on (`jomiz_jsys_lawyersys_leave_types`.id = `jomiz_jsys_lawyersys_leaves_trs`.`leave_type_id`) INNER JOIN jomiz_users on (jomiz_users.ID = `jomiz_jsys_lawyersys_leaves_trs`.`user_id`) WHERE `jomiz_jsys_lawyersys_leaves_trs`.taken > 0 AND `jomiz_jsys_lawyersys_leaves_trs`.`status` = 2 ORDER BY `start_date` ASC',
    ),
    1 => 
    (object) array(
       'permalink' => 'task-officalletter',
       'title' => 'Offical Letters',
       'template' => 'page-widget-task-officalletter.php',
       'istask' => true,
       'taskquery' => 'SELECT CONCAT( \'lawyersys/officalletter-edit?id=\', jomiz_jsys_lawyersys_officalletter.id ) AS task_link, jomiz_jsys_lawyersys_officalletter.recipient AS task_title, \'اضافة مرفق\' AS action_title, jomiz_jsys_lawyersys_officalletter.letter_date AS created_on, \'danger\' AS action_color from jomiz_jsys_lawyersys_officalletter LEFT OUTER JOIN jomiz_jsys_heap_attachments ON ( jomiz_jsys_lawyersys_officalletter.id = jomiz_jsys_heap_attachments.object_id AND jomiz_jsys_heap_attachments.object_type = \'officalletter\') GROUP by jomiz_jsys_lawyersys_officalletter.id HAVING count(jomiz_jsys_heap_attachments.id) = 0',
    ),
    2 => 
    (object) array(
       'permalink' => 'task-caseswithinweek',

       'taskquery' => 'SELECT \'lawyersys/leavesapprovals\' AS task_link, jomiz_users.display_name AS task_title, \'مغادرة/إجازة\' AS action_title, jomiz_jsys_lawyersys_leaves_trs.start_date AS created_on, \'warning\' AS action_color FROM `jomiz_jsys_lawyersys_leaves_trs` INNER JOIN `jomiz_jsys_lawyersys_leave_types` on (`jomiz_jsys_lawyersys_leave_types`.id = `jomiz_jsys_lawyersys_leaves_trs`.`leave_type_id`) INNER JOIN jomiz_users on (jomiz_users.ID = `jomiz_jsys_lawyersys_leaves_trs`.`user_id`) WHERE `jomiz_jsys_lawyersys_leaves_trs`.taken > 0 AND `jomiz_jsys_lawyersys_leaves_trs`.`status` = 2 ORDER BY `start_date` ASC',
    ),
    1 => 
    (object) array(
       'permalink' => 'task-officalletter',
       'title' => 'Offical Letters',
       'template' => 'page-widget-task-officalletter.php',
       'istask' => true,
       'taskquery' => 'SELECT CONCAT( \'lawyersys/officalletter-edit?id=\', jomiz_jsys_lawyersys_officalletter.id ) AS task_link, jomiz_jsys_lawyersys_officalletter.recipient AS task_title, \'اضافة مرفق\' AS action_title, jomiz_jsys_lawyersys_officalletter.letter_date AS created_on, \'danger\' AS action_color from jomiz_jsys_lawyersys_officalletter LEFT OUTER JOIN jomiz_jsys_heap_attachments ON ( jomiz_jsys_lawyersys_officalletter.id = jomiz_jsys_heap_attachments.object_id AND jomiz_jsys_heap_attachments.object_type = \'officalletter\') GROUP by jomiz_jsys_lawyersys_officalletter.id HAVING count(jomiz_jsys_heap_attachments.id) = 0',
    ),
    2 => 
    (object) array(
       'permalink' => 'task-caseswithinweek',

       'taskquery' => 'SELECT \'lawyersys/leavesapprovals\' AS task_link, jomiz_users.display_name AS task_title, \'مغادرة/إجازة\' AS action_title, jomiz_jsys_lawyersys_leaves_trs.start_date AS created_on, \'warning\' AS action_color FROM `jomiz_jsys_lawyersys_leaves_trs` INNER JOIN `jomiz_jsys_lawyersys_leave_types` on (`jomiz_jsys_lawyersys_leave_types`.id = `jomiz_jsys_lawyersys_leaves_trs`.`leave_type_id`) INNER JOIN jomiz_users on (jomiz_users.ID = `jomiz_jsys_lawyersys_leaves_trs`.`user_id`) WHERE `jomiz_jsys_lawyersys_leaves_trs`.taken > 0 AND `jomiz_jsys_lawyersys_leaves_trs`.`status` = 2 ORDER BY `start_date` ASC',
    ),
    1 => 
    (object) array(
       'permalink' => 'task-officalletter',
       'title' => 'Offical Letters',
       'template' => 'page-widget-task-officalletter.php',
       'istask' => true,
       'taskquery' => 'SELECT CONCAT( \'lawyersys/officalletter-edit?id=\', jomiz_jsys_lawyersys_officalletter.id ) AS task_link, jomiz_jsys_lawyersys_officalletter.recipient AS task_title, \'اضافة مرفق\' AS action_title, jomiz_jsys_lawyersys_officalletter.letter_date AS created_on, \'danger\' AS action_color from jomiz_jsys_lawyersys_officalletter LEFT OUTER JOIN jomiz_jsys_heap_attachments ON ( jomiz_jsys_lawyersys_officalletter.id = jomiz_jsys_heap_attachments.object_id AND jomiz_jsys_heap_attachments.object_type = \'officalletter\') GROUP by jomiz_jsys_lawyersys_officalletter.id HAVING count(jomiz_jsys_heap_attachments.id) = 0',
    ),
    2 => 
    (object) array(
       'permalink' => 'task-caseswithinweek',

       'taskquery' => 'SELECT \'lawyersys/leavesapprovals\' AS task_link, jomiz_users.display_name AS task_title, \'مغادرة/إجازة\' AS action_title, jomiz_jsys_lawyersys_leaves_trs.start_date AS created_on, \'warning\' AS action_color FROM `jomiz_jsys_lawyersys_leaves_trs` INNER JOIN `jomiz_jsys_lawyersys_leave_types` on (`jomiz_jsys_lawyersys_leave_types`.id = `jomiz_jsys_lawyersys_leaves_trs`.`leave_type_id`) INNER JOIN jomiz_users on (jomiz_users.ID = `jomiz_jsys_lawyersys_leaves_trs`.`user_id`) WHERE `jomiz_jsys_lawyersys_leaves_trs`.taken > 0 AND `jomiz_jsys_lawyersys_leaves_trs`.`status` = 2 ORDER BY `start_date` ASC',
    ),
    1 => 
    (object) array(
       'permalink' => 'task-officalletter',
       'title' => 'Offical Letters',
       'template' => 'page-widget-task-officalletter.php',
       'istask' => true,
       'taskquery' => 'SELECT CONCAT( \'lawyersys/officalletter-edit?id=\', jomiz_jsys_lawyersys_officalletter.id ) AS task_link, jomiz_jsys_lawyersys_officalletter.recipient AS task_title, \'اضافة مرفق\' AS action_title, jomiz_jsys_lawyersys_officalletter.letter_date AS created_on, \'danger\' AS action_color from jomiz_jsys_lawyersys_officalletter LEFT OUTER JOIN jomiz_jsys_heap_attachments ON ( jomiz_jsys_lawyersys_officalletter.id = jomiz_jsys_heap_attachments.object_id AND jomiz_jsys_heap_attachments.object_type = \'officalletter\') GROUP by jomiz_jsys_lawyersys_officalletter.id HAVING count(jomiz_jsys_heap_attachments.id) = 0',
    ),
    2 => 
    (object) array(
       'permalink' => 'task-caseswithinweek',
